Whether you need to share a quick screen recording, social media clip, or personal video, our platform provides a lightning-fast way to get your content online and in front of your audience. |

Returns RAG-ready JSON with JATS full-text chunks (cl100k_base, 512/50) when available and abstract fallback otherwise. Drop-in for LangChain, LlamaIndex, Qdrant, Pinecone, Weaviate, pgvector. $0.02 per preprint. |
